##### NEW_REVOLTERS EVENTS
### ID's 677000-699999 and on
# number 69+U-number+00-99 for U00 to U99 nations
# number 680+UA-number +00-99 for UA0 to UA9 nations
# number 681+UB-number +00-99 for UB0 to UB9 nations
# number 682+UC-number +00-99 for UC0 to UC9 nations
# number 683+UD-number +00-99 for UD0 to UD9 nations
# number 684+UE-number +00-99 for UE0 to UE9 nations
# number 685+UF-number +00-99 for UF0 to UF9 nations
# use 677000-679999 for events for normal or armageddon nations
# also use 686000-689999 for same
################################################################
# For some hypothetical nations there are no deaths, just batch
# retirements at logical times, obviating the need for death
# events. This is to reduce CPU overhead 
################################################################
event = {
	id = 677000
	random = no
	country = PAL #Palestine
	
	trigger = { 	}

	date = { day = 25  month = december year = 1941 }
	offset = 3
	deathdate = { day = 30 month = december year = 2029 }

	name = "EVT_103_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_103_DESC"
	picture = "minister_died"
	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 557028 }#George Antinous
	}
}

event = {
	id = 677008
	random = no
	country = PAL #Palestine
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			war = { country = PAL country = ENG }
			year = 1950
		}
 	}

	date = { day = 0  month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 30 month = december year = 2029 }

	name = "British Mandate Officials Retire"
	desc = "Officials who belong to the historic British mandate in Palestine are retired. This includes mostly government officials specifically listed on sites such as worldstatesmen.org., or who belong to other countries in Paradox files. Military leaders are kept for gameplay reasons."
	picture = "minister_died"
	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 557001 }#Sir Harold McMichael
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 557002 }#Sir John R. Chancellor
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 557006 }#Frederic G.Peake
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 557007 }#Sir Herbert Samuel
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 557008 }#G.H.C. Spinls

#####################################
# hypothetical Palestinian elections if democratic
#####################################
event = {
	id = 677010
	random = no
	country = PAL #Palestine
	
	trigger = { 
		OR = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			government = democratic
		}
	}

	date = { day = 14  month = may year = 1952 }

	name = "Palestinian Elections"
	desc = "Elections were held in Palestine."
	
	action_a = {
		name = "Elect Left"
		ai_chance = 30
		command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = -5 }
		command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = 7 }
		command = { type = domestic which = democratic value = 5 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -3 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "Elect Right"
		ai_chance = 30
		command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = 5 }
		command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = -7 }
		command = { type = domestic which = democratic value = 5 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -3 }
	}
	action_c = {
		name = "Keep Current Government"
		ai_chance = 37
		command = { type = dissent value = -1 }
	}
	action_d = {
		name = "Coup d'État"
		ai_chance = 3
		command = { type = domestic which = democratic value = -8 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 10 }
	}
}

	trigger = { government = democratic }

	name = "Isser Harel Head of Mossad"
	desc = "Isser Harel becomes Head of the Mossad."

	action_a = {
		name = "YES"
		ai_chance = 95
		command = { type = ministerofintelligence which = 559097 }#Harel
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "NO"
		ai_chance = 5
		command = {  }
	}
}

##########################
# Communist Greece events
##########################
event = {
	id = 680200
	random = no
	country = UA2 # Communist Greece
	
	trigger = {
		exists = GRE
		war = { country = UA2 country = GRE }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = UA2 country = SOV } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = GRE country = USA } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = GRE country = ENG } }
		control = { province = 392 }
		control = { province = 393 }
		control = { province = 394 }
		control = { province = 395 }
		control = { province = 400 }
		control = { province = 401 }
		control = { province = 402 }
		control = { province = 403 }
		control = { province = 410 }
		control = { province = 411 }
		control = { province = 412 }
		NOT = { owned = { province = 401 } }#Athens taken not owned
		control = { province = 396  data = GRE }#Crete not taken
 	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1942 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1969  }

	name = "Peace negotiations"
	desc = "The Central Committee considered and decided to present a peace plan to the Allies, leaving the Communist state in control of the Greek mainland."
	
	action_a = {
		name = "Negotiate Peace"
		ai_chance = 90
		command = { type = trigger which = 680201 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "Fight for a United Greece"
		ai_chance = 10
		command = { }
	}
}
event = {
	id = 680201
	random = no
	country = GRE # Nationalist Greece
	
	#

	name = "Peace negotiations"
	desc = "The Communist side has presented a peace plan. Although it is a disappointment to us, it leaves us in control of the vital islands in the Mediterranean."
	
	action_a = {
		name = "Accept the Plan"
		ai_chance = 50
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = UA2 value = 392 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = UA2 value = 394 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = UA2 value = 395 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = UA2 value = 401 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = UA2 value = 402 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = UA2 value = 403 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = UA2 value = 410 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = UA2 value = 411 }
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = UA2 value = 412 }
		command = { type = removecore which = 392 }
		command = { type = removecore which = 394 }
		command = { type = removecore which = 395 }
		command = { type = removecore which = 401 }
		command = { type = removecore which = 402 }
		command = { type = removecore which = 403 }
		command = { type = removecore which = 410 }
		command = { type = removecore which = 411 }
		command = { type = removecore which = 412 }
		command = { type = peace which = UA2 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 680202 }		
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "Ask the USA for help"
		ai_chance = 50
		command = { type = trigger which = 680203 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 680204 }
	}
}
event = {

		name = "OK" #Grantley Herbert Adams
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 832001 }
	}

	random = no
	country = U51 #Zambia
	style = 0
	
	trigger = {
		government = democratic
		headofstate = 851000
		headofgovernment = 851001
		random = 2
		OR = {
			exists = SOV
			exists = CHC
		}
 	}

	date = { day = 2 month = march year = 1958 }
	offset = 25
	deathdate = { day = 18 month = january year = 1999 }

	name = "Constitutional Crisis"
	desc = "Amidst complaints of excessive government power, Kenneth Kaunda abolished the post of Prime Minister, and moved to realize his vision of African Socialism in a one-party state modelled after the Soviet Union."
	picture = "parliamentary_scandal"

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = set_domestic which = democratic value = 5 }
		command = { type = set_domestic which = political_left value = 9 }
		command = { type = headofgovernment which = 851020 }
		command = { type = foreignminister which = 851021 }
		command = { type = armamentminister which = 851022 }
		command = { type = ministerofsecurity which = 851023 }
		command = { type = ministerofintelligence which = 851024 }
	}
}

		}
	}

	offset = 1

	}
}
